<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрослый.html>взро́слый</a> (8655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрослый.html>взро́слый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzróslyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)взросле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:взрослеть.html>взросле́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрослый.html>взро́слый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grown, grown-up, adult</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взрыв</a> (1772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взрыв</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взры́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взры́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взры́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>explosion</li>
<li>blast</li>
<li>detonation</li>
<li>eruption</li></ol>

***взрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a> (13624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взорвать.html>взорва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow up, to detonate, to blast
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvátʹ</b> zarjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set off a charge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enrage, to exasperate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also used impersonally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>Их</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбление.html>оскорбле́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ix <b>vzryválo</b> za oskorblénije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were boiling with rage at the insult.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрываться.html>взрыва́ться</a> (10180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрываться.html>взрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взорваться.html>взорва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow up, to detonate</li>
<li>to become enraged, to become exasperated, to explode verbally</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***взрывной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывно́й</a> (11752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взрыв</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> explosive

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывчатка.html>взрывча́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvčátka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывчатка.html>взрывча́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывчатка.html>взрывча́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывчатка.html>взрывча́ток</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́вший</a> (10717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***взывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a> (10717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with reduction of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*взз-</span> to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вз-</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвать.html>воззва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appeal <i>(to someone for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyvátʹ</b> o pómošči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call for help</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:справедливость.html>справедли́вости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyvátʹ</b> o spravedlívosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demand justice</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***взыграть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыграть.html>взыгра́ть</a> (28087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыграть.html>взыгра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzygrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взы́грывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start frolicking, to jump for joy</li>
<li>to swell <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the sea, wind, a river, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manifest strongly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a feeling</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to swell <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of pride</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to leap <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzyskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyskánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>penalty, punishment

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуться.html>подве́ргнуться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́нию</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvérgnutʹsja <b>vzyskániju</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">incur a penalty</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>recovery, exaction

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>долга́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyskánije</b> dolgá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">recovery of debt</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***взыскать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a> (16699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>иска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взы́скивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exact <i>(from, of)</i>, to recover <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyskátʹ</b> dolg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recover a debt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make answer <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыщи́те</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vzyščíte!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">please forgive me!; don't be hard on me!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzyskánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***взять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> (138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъzęti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взимать.html>взима́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взыма́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмом</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzjatʹ</b> štúrmom štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to take</b> something by storm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzjatʹ</b> k sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вместе.html>вме́сте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взятый.html>взя́тых</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vméste <b>vzjátyx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">put together, combined</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***взяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́ться</a> (1176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:браться.html>бра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take something with hands, to take (mutually, together) (e.g. each other's hands)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>Возьмёмся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзья́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поодиночке.html>поодино́чке</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vozʹmjómsja</b> zá ruki, druzʹjá, štob ne propástʹ poodinóčke.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's <b>take</b> each other's hands, my friends, so that we don't perish one by one.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>Bulat Okudzhava</i>, a song)</dd></dl></li>
<li>to set about; to undertake (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative case <i>a task</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льника</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>возьму́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S ponedélʹnika <b>vozʹmúsʹ</b> za anglíjskij jazýk.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">From Monday I'll <b>tackle</b> English.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appear, to emerge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:откуда.html>отку́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>возьму́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli ne xvatájet déneg sevódnja, otkúda oní <b>vozʹmútsja</b> závtra?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If there's not enough money today, where will it <b>come from</b> tomorrow?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***вибрировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вибрировать.html>вибри́ровать</a> (14813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вибрировать.html>вибри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vibrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завибрировать.html>завибри́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to vibrate, to oscillate</li>
<li>to quaver</li>
<li>to shimmy</li>
<li>to thrill</li>
<li>to flutter</li>
<li>to jar</li>
<li>to pulsate</li>
<li>to chatter</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вибра́тор</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vibrátor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
